The young, energetic candidate who had promised to build a bridge to the 21st century was now a man weighed down by defeats and mistakes, real and perceived. You were confident, maybe too confident. You’d told yourself that the debates had gone well, that the voters cared more about jobs and health care than your personal life. But in the end, you weren’t been able to overcome the relentless drumbeat of Republican attacks or the weariness of an electorate ready for change.

You made a simple speech about accepting the results of the election, and continuing the fight, even outside of the Oval Office. Although the crowd cheered, you felt as if it was almost out of pity. You still felt like there was work to do, and that the American people cut you short.                   " } return construct(0); } } /* Welcome to Astro's Variable Headquarters This is a fairly simple function you can add to your mods. It will create a little menu in which the player can view the numbers laid out within the functions. This is a great way to give the player a little more information about your mod. Across this code, you will find a lot of aspects you can edit. I have left plenty of comments to help you understand what each part does. Don't be afraid to ask in #mod-help on the Discord for clarification or help with editing this code. To use this, place this code below your Code 2, and edit it as needed. You can duplicate the 'let a = document.createElement('p');' section to add more lines of text. Functions are referenced in text like so: ' + function + '. This will display the number from the function in the text. Credit to Nina, who made the original code that summoned the new screen (originally for the 1960Red/1952Blue advisor screen) Go ahead and use this code in your mods - just give me credit. I hope it helps you out! */ e =campaignTrail_temp let loopingSound; // Declare loopingSound globally // Load the sound const errorSound = new Audio('https://audio.jukehost.co.uk/kCQEFsusfQmaqunaLbrSlyej5we0tGJF'); // Global error handler window.onerror = function (message, source, lineno, colno, error) { // Play the error sound if (errorSound.paused) { errorSound.loop = true; errorSound.play(); audio.pause(); } // Log the error for debugging console.error(`Error occurred: ${message} at ${source}:${lineno}:${colno}`); // Optionally, notify the user alert("An error occurred. Please check the console for details."); // Return true to prevent the default error handler return true; }; // Optional: Stop the sound after debugging is done window.onkeydown = function (event) { if (event.key === "Escape") { // Stop on pressing "Escape" errorSound.pause(); errorSound.currentTime = 0; // Reset playback } }; function addHeadquarterButton() { // Check if the button already exists if (document.getElementById('headquarter_button')) { return; } // Find the reference button by its ID const refButton = document.getElementById('view_electoral_map'); if (!refButton) { return; } // Create a new button element const newButton = document.createElement('button'); newButton.id = 'headquarter_button'; newButton.style.marginLeft = '1.5em'; newButton.innerHTML = 'Personal Computer'; const newButtonSound = new Audio('https://audio.jukehost.co.uk/tO2cWkdv5h3DD6m6KQytiK5UEv1l9PaJ'); // Replace with actual sound path // Attach the click event listener newButton.addEventListener('click', function () { // Show the pixelated loading screen showLoadingScreen(); // Pause the current soundtrack const audio = document.getElementById("audio"); audio.pause(); // Play the Campaign Data sound effect newButtonSound.play(); // Once the sound is finished, start looping sound newButtonSound.onended = function () { if (!loopingSound) { loopingSound = new Audio('https://audio.jukehost.co.uk/e19IDfLbWvkktOmCzyC4s54Aj8g75CZI'); } loopingSound.loop = true; loopingSound.play(); console.log('Campaign sound ended, starting loop'); }; // Load the macBackground function after 3 seconds (when the loading screen ends) setTimeout(() => { hideLoadingScreen(); macBackground(); }, 3000); // 3 seconds }); // Insert the new button next to the reference button refButton.insertAdjacentElement('afterend', newButton); } // Function to show the pixelated loading screen function showLoadingScreen() { let loadingOverlay = document.createElement('div'); loadingOverlay.id = 'loadingOverlay'; loadingOverlay.style.position = 'fixed'; loadingOverlay.style.top = '0'; loadingOverlay.style.left = '0'; loadingOverlay.style.width = '100%'; loadingOverlay.style.height = '100%'; loadingOverlay.style.backgroundColor = 'black'; // Old computer screens were often black loadingOverlay.style.color = 'green'; // Typical green text on old screens loadingOverlay.style.fontFamily = '"Press Start 2P", monospace'; // Pixelated font loadingOverlay.style.fontSize = '20px'; loadingOverlay.style.zIndex = '10000'; loadingOverlay.style.display = 'flex'; loadingOverlay.style.alignItems = 'center'; loadingOverlay.style.justifyContent = 'center'; loadingOverlay.style.flexDirection = 'column'; loadingOverlay.innerHTML = `
                  `; document.body.appendChild(loadingOverlay); } // Function to hide the loading screen function hideLoadingScreen() { const loadingOverlay = document.getElementById('loadingOverlay'); if (loadingOverlay) { loadingOverlay.remove(); } } let draggablePic; // Global variable for headquarters image let minsweeperPic; // Global variable for minsweeper image function macBackground() { // Create and set up a full-page background container let bgContainer = document.createElement('div'); bgContainer.id = 'bgContainer'; bgContainer.style.position = 'fixed'; bgContainer.style.top = '0'; bgContainer.style.left = '0'; bgContainer.style.width = '100%'; bgContainer.style.height = '100%'; bgContainer.style.backgroundImage = 'url(https://i.imgur.com/gpdpc72.png)'; bgContainer.style.backgroundSize = 'cover'; bgContainer.style.backgroundPosition = 'center'; bgContainer.style.zIndex = '999'; document.body.appendChild(bgContainer); // Create the draggable picture element for Headquarters let draggablePic = document.createElement('img'); draggablePic.src = 'https://i.imgur.com/hbT1unU.png'; draggablePic.style.position = 'fixed'; draggablePic.style.right = '20px'; draggablePic.style.top = '40%'; draggablePic.style.transform = 'translateY(-50%)'; draggablePic.style.cursor = 'pointer'; draggablePic.style.zIndex = '1000'; document.body.appendChild(draggablePic); // Make the image draggable makeDraggable(draggablePic); // Add click event to trigger openHeadquarters function draggablePic.addEventListener('click', openHeadquarter); // Add event listener to make draggablePic visible when clicked draggablePic.addEventListener('click', function() { cnnContent.style.display = 'none'; // Show the draggablePic element hqContent.style.display = 'block'; // Show the draggablePic element }); // Create the draggable picture element for minsweeper let minsweeperPic = document.createElement('img'); minsweeperPic.src = 'https://i.imgur.com/WHvQ8KI.png'; minsweeperPic.style.position = 'fixed'; minsweeperPic.style.left = '20px'; minsweeperPic.style.top = '40%'; minsweeperPic.style.transform = 'translateY(-50%)'; minsweeperPic.style.cursor = 'pointer'; minsweeperPic.style.zIndex = '1000'; document.body.appendChild(minsweeperPic); // Make the image draggable makeDraggable(minsweeperPic); // Add click event to trigger minsweeper window minsweeperPic.addEventListener('click', openMinesweeper); // Create the "Close Mac" button let closeMacButton = document.createElement('button'); closeMacButton.textContent = 'Close Mac'; closeMacButton.style.position = 'fixed'; closeMacButton.style.top = '10px'; closeMacButton.style.left = '10px'; closeMacButton.style.zIndex = '1001'; // Make sure it's above the other elements document.body.appendChild(closeMacButton); // Add event listener to the "Close Mac" button closeMacButton.addEventListener('click', function() { // Show the confirmation box let confirmClose = confirm("Do you want to close your mac?"); if (confirmClose) { // If the user chooses "Yes", hide everything if (loopingSound) { console.log("Attempting to stop the looping sound..."); // Stop the looping sound loopingSound.pause(); // Pause the sound loopingSound.currentTime = 0; // Reset the time to the beginning // Ensure it is not looping anymore loopingSound.loop = false; // Disable the loop // Forcefully stop the sound if it's still playing if (!loopingSound.paused) { console.log("Sound was playing, forcing stop..."); // Debugging loopingSound.pause(); // Pause the sound again loopingSound.currentTime = 0; // Reset to the beginning } else { console.log("Sound already paused."); // Debugging } } else { console.log("No looping sound to stop."); let match; while ((match = regex.exec(str)) !== null) { matches.push({ start: match.index + (match[0].startsWith('“') ? 1 : 0), // Adjust for potential starting “ end: match.index + match[0].length - (match[0].endsWith('”') ? 1 : 0) - (match[2] ? 1 : 0), tooltipIndex: index }); } }); // Sort by starting position; if two start at the same position, longer match comes first matches.sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start || b.end - b.start - (a.end - a.start)); // Filter out overlaps for (let i = 0; i < matches.length - 1; ) { if (matches[i + 1].start < matches[i].end) { matches.splice(i + 1, 1); // Remove the next match since it overlaps } else { i++; // Move to next match } } return matches; } function applyTooltips(str) { const matches = getTooltips(str); let result = ''; let lastIndex = 0; matches.forEach(match => { const tooltip = tooltipList[match.tooltipIndex]; result += str.slice(lastIndex, match.start); result += `${tooltip.searchString}${tooltip.explanationText}`; lastIndex = match.end; }); result += str.slice(lastIndex); // Add the remainder of the original string return result; } function applyTooltipsToObject(obj) { for (let key in obj) { if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') { obj[key] = applyTooltips(obj[key]); } else if (typeof obj[key] === 'object') { applyTooltipsToObject(obj[key]); // Recursive call } } } function modifytooltip(searchstring, newtooltip) { for (let x in tooltipList) { if (tooltipList[x]["searchString"] == searchstring) { tooltipList[x]["explanationText"] = newtooltip; }; } } applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.questions_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answers_json); applyTooltipsToObject(campaignTrail_temp.answer_feedback_json); function question_insert(insertafter_pk,question) { let foundpk = false; for (x in campaignTrail_temp.questions_json) { if (campaignTrail_temp.questions_json[x]["pk"] == insertafter_pk && foundpk == false) { campaignTrail_temp.questions_json.splice(Number(x)+1,0,question); foundpk = true; } } if (foundpk == false) { console.log("PK not found! "+insertafter_pk); } }
